(Person Served) met in our Newton Outpatient Center to discuss the importance of continued funding for Medicaid. Vic: Making your individual voice heard is important, but collective action is always more successful than unilateral advocacy. Advocacy coalitions, whether formal or informal, bring increased attention to relevant issues, and their greater numbers make policymakers more responsive.
